 Book Review: 2014 The Election That Changed India (english) Author: Rajdeep sardesaipublisher: Viking, Penguin publicationseducation: Hard Bound, 372 pages Price: Rs 599 This book by senior TV journalist Rajdeep Sardesai has been written keeping the 2014 Lok Sabha elections at the center
 is chunavi jang main nayak or vijeta banakar ubhare bijepi ke narendra modi
 Rahul Gandhi of Congress or charitra abhinayta banakar twist laane kii koshish karte rahe aam aadmi party ke arvind kejariwal
 Sardesai has woven the entire plot based on three types of workplaces and stories under the pretext of these three persons
 is kitaab kii khoobiyonper charchaa sabase pehle
 The book does not spread linguistic confusion
 aapaki agar raajnneeti main jaraa bhi dilchaspee he to ise silsilewar dhang se pard sakate hai
 Its second quality is consistency
 kitaab main i-campan se lekar, khaas reliyon tak, naaron se lekar vaadon tak, ranneetik galatiyon se lekar master stroke tak, lagbhag har ek daanv kii kahani bayaan kii gai he
 The third feature of the book is some stories, which Rajdeep has evidently told based on his experience
 isamen times nau channel par rahul gandhi ke charchit intervyuu se pehle barkhaa dutt kii koshishon kaa kissa ho yaa phir india tivi ke program aapaki adaalat main modi ke aane kaa kissa
 Or else Kejriwal's resignation without consulting the colleagues
 iske alaava rajdeep ne teenon hi netaaon, modi, gandhi or kejariwal ke saath apane nijee anubhav saajha kiye
 Shared his understanding of his politics
 iske chalate kitaab raajnneetik uthapatak kaa khalis shastreey varnan nahin rah jaati
 Another feature of the book is the interesting figures and facts related to the Lok Sabha elections given at the end
 is baar ke loksabhaa chunaav kai maamalon main nae the
 Use social media or selective interviewing strategy
 piem candidet kii chhavi ke ird gird chunaav hon yaa phir congress kaa puri tarah se rahul gandhi ke kamjor kandhon par tikaa hona
 For 10 years, a pm-turned man has to be more or less a mute spectator in this power struggle, or a party formed a few years ago due to media hype, or Kejriwal's poll stunt challenging Modi in Benaras
 har din nai bisaat bichaai ja rahi thi
 New pots were being created
 nae or apratyaashit dhang se hamale kiye ja rahe the
 In the midst of all this, India gave a clear and in many cases unprecedented mandate
 rajdeep kii yah kitabais janadesh ke kai baarik pahalu samajhane main madad karti he
 It also takes a critical look at Modi's political journey
 kis tarah dilli main sanghathan kii siyasat karata ek shaks dedh dashak main desh kii aakankshaon kaa centre ban gaya
 Since Modi is the winner, it is evident that his methods and strategies got the most place in the book
 iske baad number aayaa congress or kejariwal kaa
 In the book, Rajdeep also spoke on the difficulties of the TV journalist's profession and all the doubts that arose about the exit poll
 kitaab main kuch kamiyaan bhi lageen
 Rajdeep's identity has been a clear stand on all controversial issues
 vah kuch logon ko raas aata he, to kuch ko nahin
 But here, due to the mandate, he may be seen as being generous but not in the comments in many places
 gujarat dangon main modi kii kathith bhoomika ho yaa farji muthbhed ke maamalon main bijepi adhyaksh amit shah par aarope
 The author said on the lines of 'let the past tame, let the future be improved', but it was not perfect
 isi tarah cash for vot cond ke dauraan kiye gaye sting oparation main bhi vah apane hisse kaa sach bataate samay bahut kanvising nahin lagate

 How Narendra Modi won this election, the book tells it in a very fashionable way, but it does not go very deep on why it won
 rajdeep khud ko yah kahkar bari bhi karte hai ki main koi raajnneeti vigyaan kaa gyaata nahin
 But i am a reporter
 jameen par jo dekha, suna, bas use hi bataa rahaa hum
 Those who have followed the Lok Sabha elections very closely

 Is the oldest person in the world in India? If the claims of feroz-un-din Mir, who lives in Kashmir, are to be believed, the answer is yes
 mir kaa daawa he ki wo 141 saal ke hai
 If this thing turns out to be true, then he will be the oldest person in the world
 daily mail ke mutabik, mir kaa kahana he ki unke paas sarkari certificate bhi he jisamen unki umr 10 march 1872 likhi he
 It is believed that Guinness World Records can now investigate his claim
 philhal duniya ke sabase umradraj vyakti hone kaa record misaao okava ke naam darj he, jinaki umr 115 saal he
 If Mir's claims are found to be true, he may even leave behind the French woman Jean Calment, who set the record for the longest survival
 camelent kii maut 122 saal kii umr main saal 1997 main ho gai thi
 According to Kashmir Life's report, Mir can still walk with the help of his family
 yahi nahin vah apni jindagi kii kahani bhi bayaan karte hai
 Mir used to trade fruits and dry fruits like his father
 saal 1890 main unhone shaadi kii
 He remained in Pakistan with his first wife till 1900
 patni kii maut ke baad ve bharat aa gaye
 According to Mir, 'at that time there was no border between India and Pakistan
 mujaffarabad janaa srinagar jane se zyada aasaan tha
 i used to work in Karachi with a business family who used to buy nuts from me
 main mewa kashmir se laata tha, jo karachi main bahut mashhoor the
 'when his first wife died, he moved to his birth place Bhijma village in Uri district of Kashmir

 But people who drink tea daily are probably unaware of other benefits and uses of tea
 chaay aapako taazgi dene ke saath or bhi bahut kuch de sakati he
 Know these 9 benefits of tea 
 
 1
 Keep the hair shiny If you want good shine in the hair, then use green tea
 haalanki yah usee ped se banati he, jisase kaali chaay aati he
 But the way to make it is different
 green tii ko oxidise nahin kiya jaataa, jiske chalate isaki pattiyon main electron kii sankhya zyada hoti he
 These electrons give shine to your hair
 aise karen istemaal:green tii ke teen bag, ek jag uble pani main daalen or thanda hone ke liye chhod den
 When cool, remove the tea bag and wash the hair with that water
 10 minute baad baalo main condishnar lagaaein
 Now you will see the shine of hair
 aap baalo ko dark bhi kar sakate hai
 You just have to use black tea instead of green
 2
 Make eyes beautiful If your eyes are swollen a little, then there is no need to worry
 istemaal kiye hue do tii bag aapaki samasya hal kar sakate hai
 Stress, allergies, excessive drinking or hormonal changes can cause eye inflammation
 lekin chaay main maujuud caffeine, suji hui khun kii nason ko skin main dabaa degi or aapaki ankhen puri tarah thik ho jaaengi
 Here's how to use: Take two used T-bags and close your eyes and keep them on top
 10 minute tak rakhane ke baad unhen hataaen
 Now your eyes will be fresh
 3
 Clean the dirty carpet in minutes
 If the carpet in your house is dirty, then with the help of tea you can clean it well
 thodi-si khuli chaay len or use karpet par halki-si parat ke rup main failaa den
 Now pour some water over the kettle and rub it in the carpet
 15 minute baad use farsh se hataaen
 Now the dust and smell of the carpet will be gone
 4
 Save from Sun Burn When you have to stay in the sun for a long time and you cannot avoid it, then it is inevitable to get marks of sunburn on your face
 aise main thande tii-bag len or jis jagah par skin prabhavit hui he, vahaan 10 minute tak rakhen
 The effect will be seen immediately
 5
 Remove shaving rash in a pinch
 If you have shaving rash on your underarms or feet, use a tea bag
 shaving ke baad paanch minute tak arms ke neeche pani main bhigaa tii-bag dabaakar rakhen
 This will protect your skin from shaving rash, which results from a bad blade
 agar ek baar main zyada hissaa cover karnaa chaahate hai, to chaay ko ek kapade main lapet len or phir istemaal karen
 6
 chaay kii pattee se khilenge gulabchay kii pattee main paaya janaa vaala tannic acid gulab ke rang ko or sundar kar detaa he
 Tear off the used T-bag and scatter it around the root of the rose
 yah ped kii jadon se milakar phulon ko kaaphi sundar bana detii he
 7
 injection kaa dard hoga doobgar aapaki skin thodi hard he, to injection lagane se pehle us jagah par thanda tii-bag rakhen
 After a while, the skin will become very soft and the effect of the injection will not be known at all
 saath hi kisi tarah kaa infections hone kaa khatra bhi nahin hoga
 8
 pairon ko bhi banaaen sundar or frewegar dinabhar kaam karne ke baad aapke pairon se thodi gandh aane lagati he yaa skin main kuch samasya hoti he, to phikr karne kii jarurat nahin he

 gunagune pani main tii-bag daalen or halkaa thanda hone par pairon ko usamen bhigoen
